  983     /* TEMP_MPC_FORM Summary of this function goes here */
  984     /*    Detailed explanation goes here */
  985     /*    This function formulates all the matrices for MPC QP */
  986     /*    states: current robot states, include CoM states and foot placement */
  987     /*    Nodes: Number of nodes in MPC prediction */
  988     /*    r: radius for obstacle avoidance */
  989     /*    qo: obstacle states */
  990     /*    states_ref: desired robot states */
  991     /*    MPC_index : left/right step index, contact sequence index */
  992     /*    weights   : weight in the MPC cost function */
  993     /*  unpack inputs */
  994     i0 = r1->size[0] * r1->size[1];
  995     r1->size[0] = 1;
  996     if (!(Nodes >= 0.0)) {
  997       emlrtNonNegativeCheckR2012b(Nodes, (emlrtDCInfo *)&b_emlrtDCI, sp);
